<a name="v472"></a> 
## <a name="introducing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-120">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Tanıtımı</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-120">Introducing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-121">.NET Framework'ün önceki sürümlerinde .NET Framework 4.7.2 derlemeler çok kararlı bir ürün kalan sırasında birçok yeni düzeltmeler ve çeşitli yeni özellikler ekleyerek 4.x.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-121">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 builds on previous versions of the .NET Framework 4.x by adding many new fixes and several new features while remaining a very stable product.</span></span>

### <a name="downloading-and-installing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-122">.NET Framework 4.7.2 yükleyip</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-122">Downloading and installing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-123">.NET Framework 4.7.2 aşağıdaki konumlardan yükleyebilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-123">You can download the .NET Framework 4.7.2  from the following locations:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-124">.NET framework 4.7.2 Web yükleyicisi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-124">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Web Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863262)

- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 çevrimdışı yükleyici</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 Offline Installer</span></span>](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863265)

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-126">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1 ve Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1 ile başlayarak karşılık gelen sunucu platformları yüklenebilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-126">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 can be installed on Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1, and the corresponding server platforms starting with Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-127">.NET Framework 4.7.2 web yükleyicisi veya çevrimdışı yükleyici kullanarak yükleyebilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-127">You can install the .NET Framework 4.7.2 by using either the web installer or the offline installer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-128">Çoğu kullanıcı için önerilen yol, web yükleyicisi kullanmaktır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-128">The recommended way for most users is to use the web installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-129">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Visual Studio 2012'de veya yükleyerek daha sonra hedef [4.7.2 .NET Framework Geliştirici paketi](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-129">You can target the .NET Framework 4.7.2 in Visual Studio 2012 or later by installing the [.NET Framework 4.7.2 Developer Pack](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span></span> 

### <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-130">.NET Framework 4.7.2 yenilikler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-130">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-131">.NET Framework 4.7.2 aşağıdaki alanlarda yeni özellikler içerir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-131">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-132">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-132">Core</span></span>](#core472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-133">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-133">ASP.NET</span></span>](#asp-net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-134">Ağ oluşturma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-134">Networking</span></span>](#net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-135">SQL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-135">SQL</span></span>](#sql472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-136">WPF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-136">WPF</span></span>](#wpf472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-137">ClickOnce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-137">ClickOnce</span></span>](#ClickOnce472)

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-138">.NET Framework 4.7.2 devam ediliyor odakta yardımcı teknoloji kullanıcılar için uygun bir deneyim sağlamak üzere bir uygulamanın sağlayan iyileştirilmiş Erişilebilirlik ' dir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-138">A continuing focus in the .NET Framework 4.7.2 is improved accessibility, which allows an application to provide an appropriate experience for users of Assistive Technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-139">.NET Framework'teki 4.7.2 erişilebilirlik geliştirme hakkında daha fazla bilgi için bkz: [erişilebilirlik .NET Framework'teki yenilikler](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-139">For information on accessibility improvement in the .NET Framework 4.7.2, see [What's new in accessibility in the .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span></span> 

<a name="core-472" />
#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-140">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-140">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-141">.NET Framework 4.7.2 çok sayıda şifreleme geliştirmelerinden, ZIP arşivini ve ek koleksiyon API'leri daha iyi sıkıştırmayı desteği sunar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-141">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 features a large number of cryptographic enhancements, better decompression support for ZIP archives, and additional collection APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-142">**RSA yeni aşırı. Oluşturma ve DSA. Oluşturma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-142">**New overloads of RSA.Create and DSA.Create**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-143"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> Ve <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemleri sağlayan yeni bir örneği anahtar parametreleri sağlamanıza <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> veya <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> anahtarı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-143">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you supply key parameters when instantiated a new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-144">Kod aşağıdaki gibi değiştirin olanak sağlar:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-144">They allow you to replace code like the following:</span></span>

```csharp
// Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create())
{
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters);
   // Other code to execute using the RSA instance.
}
``` 

```vb
' Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create()
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
``` 
<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-145">koduyla şuna benzer:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-145">with code like this:</span></span>
```csharp
// Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters))
{
   // Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
}
``` 
```vb
' Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
``` 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-146"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> Ve <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemleri yeni oluşturmanıza izin <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> veya <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> anahtarlarını belirli bir anahtar boyutuna sahip.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-146">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you generate new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> keys with a specific key size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-147">Örneğin:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-147">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
using (DSA dsa = DSA.Create(2048))
{
   // Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
}
``` 
```vb
Using dsa = DSA.Create(2048)
   ' Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
End Using
``` 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-148">**Rfc2898DeriveBytes oluşturucular bir karma algoritması adı kabul edin**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-148">**Rfc2898DeriveBytes constructors accept a hash algorithm name**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-149"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> Sınıfına sahip üç yeni oluşturucularla bir <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> anahtarları türetilirken kullanmak için HMAC algoritması tanımlayan parametresi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-149">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> class has three new constructors with a <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> parameter that identifies the HMAC algorithm to use when deriving keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-150">SHA-1 kullanmak yerine, geliştiricilerin gibi SHA-256, SHA-2 tabanlı bir HMAC aşağıdaki örnekte gösterildiği gibi kullanmanız gerekir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-150">Instead of using SHA-1, developers should use a SHA-2-based HMAC like SHA-256, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

```csharp
private static byte[] DeriveKey(string password, out int iterations, out byte[] salt, 
                                out HashAlgorithmName algorithm)
{
   iterations = 100000;
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256;

   const int SaltSize = 32;
   const int DerivedValueSize = 32;

   using (Rfc2898DeriveBytes pbkdf2 = new Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize, 
                                                             iterations, algorithm))
   {
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt;
      return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize);
   }
} 
```
```vb
Private Shared Function DeriveKey(password As String, ByRef iterations As Integer, 
                                  ByRef salt AS Byte(), ByRef algorithm As HashAlgorithmName) As Byte()
   iterations = 100000
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256

   Const SaltSize As Integer = 32
   Const  DerivedValueSize As Integer = 32

   Using pbkdf2 = New Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize, iterations, algorithm)
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt
      Return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize)
   End Using
End Function 
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-151">**Kısa ömürlü anahtarları desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-151">**Support for ephemeral keys**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-152">PFX alma, sabit sürücü atlayarak bellekten doğrudan özel anahtarları isteğe bağlı olarak yükleyebilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-152">PFX import can optionally load private keys directly from memory, bypassing the hard drive.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-153">Zaman yeni <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> bayrağı belirtilen bir <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> Oluşturucusu veya aşırı biri <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemi, özel anahtarların kısa ömürlü anahtarları olarak yüklenecektir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-153">When the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> flag is specified in an <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> constructor or one of the overloads of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method, the private keys will be loaded as ephemeral keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-154">Bu, anahtarları diskte görünür olmasını engeller.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-154">This prevents the keys from being visible on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-155">Ancak:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-155">However:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-156">Bu bayrak anahtarları diske ile yüklenen sertifikaların kalıcı değildir bu yana bir X509Store eklemek için iyi bir aday değildir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-156">Since the keys are not persisted to disk, certificates loaded with this flag are not good candidates to add to an X509Store.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-157">Bu şekilde yüklenen anahtarları neredeyse her zaman Windows CNG yüklenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-157">Keys loaded in this manner are almost always loaded via Windows CNG.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-158">Bu nedenle, arayanlar özel anahtarı genişletme yöntemleri çağırarak erişmeniz gerekir [sertifika. GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-158">Therefore, callers must access the private key by calling extension methods, such as [cert.GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-159"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> Özelliği çalışmaz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-159">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not function.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-160">Eski itibaren <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> özelliği sertifikalarla çalışmaz, geliştiricilerin kısa ömürlü anahtarları değiştirmeden önce ciddi testler gerçekleştirmesi gerektiğini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-160">Since the legacy <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not work with certificates, developers should perform rigorous testing before switching to ephemeral keys.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-161">**PKCS #10 sertifika imzalama istekleri X.509 ortak anahtar sertifikaları ve program oluşturma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-161">**Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-162">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile başlayarak, iş yüklerini varolan araç içine hazırlanan sertifika isteği oluşturma sağlayan isteği (CSR) imzalama sertifikası oluşmasına neden olabilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-162">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, workloads can generate certificate signing requests (CSRs), which allows certificate request generation to be staged into existing tooling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-163">Bu, genellikle testi senaryolarında yararlıdır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-163">This is frequently useful in test scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-164">Daha fazla bilgi ve kod örnekleri için bkz: "programlı oluşturulmasını PKCS #10 sertifika imzalama istekleri ve X.509 ortak anahtar sertifikaları" içinde [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-164">For more information and code examples, see "Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates" in the [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-165">**Yeni SignerInfo üyeler**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-165">**New SignerInfo members**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-166">4.7.2, .NET Framework ile başlayan <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> sınıfı imza hakkında daha fazla bilgi sunar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-166">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> class exposes more information about the signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-167">Değerini almak <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> imzalayan tarafından kullanılan imza algoritmasını belirlemek için özellik.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-167">You can retrieve the value of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> property to determine the signature algorithm used by the signer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> Bu imzalayan için şifreleme imzası bir kopyasını almak için çağrılabilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> can be called to get a copy of the cryptographic signature for this signer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-169">**Sarmalanan bir akış CryptoStream bırakıldıktan sonra açık bırakın**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-169">**Leaving a wrapped stream open after CryptoStream is disposed**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-170">4.7.2, .NET Framework ile başlayan <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> sınıfına sahip izin veren bir ek Oluşturucu <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> Sarmalanan akışı kapatılamadı değil.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-170">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> class has an additional constructor that allows <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> to not close the wrapped stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-171">Sarmalanan akış sonra açık kalma <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> örneği kapatılır, yeni çağrı <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> şekilde Oluşturucusu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-171">To leave the wrapped stream open after the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> instance is disposed, call the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> constructor as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var cStream = new CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen: true);
```
```vb
Dim cStream = New CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen:=true)
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-172">**DeflateStream açma değişiklikleri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-172">**Decompression changes in DeflateStream**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-173">.NET Framework 4.7.2, açma işlemleri uyarlamasını başlayarak <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> sınıfı, varsayılan olarak yerel Windows API'ları kullanmak üzere değişti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-173">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the implementation of decompression operations in the <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> class has changed to use native Windows APIs by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-174">Genellikle, bu bir önemli performans iyileştirme sonuçlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-174">Typically, this results in a substantial performance improvement.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-175">Windows API'leri kullanarak açma desteği, .NET Framework 4.7.2 hedefleyen uygulamalar için varsayılan olarak etkindir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-175">Support for decompression by using Windows APIs is enabled by default for applications that target .NET Framework 4.7.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-176">.NET Framework'ün önceki sürümlerini hedefleyen ama .NET Framework 4.7.2 altında çalışan uygulamalar kabul Bu davranış aşağıdaki ekleyerek [AppContext anahtar](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) uygulama yapılandırma dosyası için:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-176">Applications that target earlier versions of .NET Framework but are running under .NET Framework 4.7.2 can opt into this behavior by adding the following [AppContext switch](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) to the application configuration file:</span></span>

```xml
<AppContextSwitchOverrides value="Switch.System.IO.Compression.DoNotUseNativeZipLibraryForDecompression=false" /> 
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-177">**Ek koleksiyon API'leri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-177">**Additional collection APIs**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-178">.NET Framework 4.7.2 bir dizi yeni API ekler <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> ve <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> türleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-178">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a number of new APIs to the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> and <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-179">Bu güncelleştirmeler şunlardır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-179">These include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-180">`TryGetValue` diğer koleksiyon türleri bu iki türü için kullanılan deneyin düzeni genişletme yöntemleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-180">`TryGetValue` methods, which extend the try pattern used in other collection types to these two types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-181">Yöntemler şunlardır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-181">The methods are:</span></span>
   - [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-182">' ortak bool Hashset'i<T>. TryGetValue (T equalValue, T actualValue çıkışı);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-182">\`public bool HashSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-183">' ortak bool SortedSet<T>. TryGetValue (T equalValue, T actualValue çıkışı);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-183">\`public bool SortedSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue);</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)
- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-184">`Enumerable.To*` bir koleksiyona Dönüştür genişletme yöntemleri bir <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-184">`Enumerable.To*` extension methods, which convert a collection to a <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span></span>
   - [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-185">ortak statik Hashset'i<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Bu IEnumerable<TSource> kaynak);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-185">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source);</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-186">ortak statik Hashset'i<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Bu IEnumerable<TSource> kaynağı, IEqualityComparer<TSource> karşılaştırıcı);</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-186">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source, IEqualityComparer<TSource> comparer);</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)
- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-187">Yeni <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> olanak tanıyan oluşturucuları ayarlayın performans avantajı boyutunu bildiğiniz durumlarda veren koleksiyonunun kapasite <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> önceden:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-187">New <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> constructors that let you set the collection's capacity, which yields a performance benefit when you know the size of the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> in advance:</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-188">[Ortak Hashset'i (int Kapasite)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-188">[public HashSet(int capacity)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-189">[Ortak Hashset'i (int kapasite, IEqualityComparer<T> karşılaştırıcı)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-189">[public HashSet(int capacity, IEqualityComparer<T> comparer)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span></span>  

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-190"><xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> Sınıfı içeren yeni aşırı <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> ve <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> yöntemlerinin sözlükten bir değer almak için ya da onu bulunmazsa ve eklemek için sözlük veya zaten varsa güncelleştirmek için bir değer ekleyin.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-190">The <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> class includes new overloads of the <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> and <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> methods to retrieve a value from the dictionary or to add it if it is not found, and to add a value to the dictionary or to update it if it already exists.</span></span>

```csharp
public TValue AddOrUpdate<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> addValueFactory, Func<TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue> updateValueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)

public TValue GetOrAdd<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> valueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)
```

```vb
Public AddOrUpdate(Of TArg)(key As TKey, addValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), updateValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue

Public GetOrAdd(Of TArg)(key As TKey, valueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue
```

<a name="asp-net472" />
#### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-191">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-191">ASP.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-192">**Web Forms bağımlılık ekleme desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-192">**Support for dependency injection in Web Forms**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-193">[Bağımlılık ekleme (dı)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#what-is-dependency-injection) nesnenin kod artık yalnızca bir bağımlılık değiştiği için değiştirilmesi gerekir böylece nesneler ve onların bağımlılıkları ayrıştırır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-193">[Dependency injection (DI)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#what-is-dependency-injection) decouples objects and their dependencies so that an object's code no longer needs to be changed just because a dependency has changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-194">.NET Framework 4.7.2 hedefleyen ASP.NET uygulamaları geliştirirken, şunları yapabilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-194">When developing ASP.NET applications that target the .NET Framework 4.7.2, you can:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-195">Ayarlayıcı, arabirim ve Oluşturucusu tabanlı yerleştirmeye kullanmak [işleyicileri ve modülleri](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [sayfasında örnekleri](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), ve [kullanıcı denetimleri](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) ASP.NET web uygulaması projeleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-195">Use setter-based, interface-based, and constructor-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) of ASP.NET web application projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-196">Ayarlayıcı ve arabirim tabanlı yerleştirmeye kullanmak [işleyicileri ve modülleri](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [sayfasında örnekleri](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), ve [kullanıcı denetimleri](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) ASP.NET web sitesi projeleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-196">Use setter-based and interface-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/bb398986.aspx), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/y6wb1a0e.aspx) of ASP.NET web site projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-197">İçinde farklı bağımlılık ekleme çerçeve takın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-197">Plug in different dependency injection frameworks.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-198">**Aynı sitede tanımlama bilgileri için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-198">**Support for same-site cookies**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) bir tarayıcı tanımlama bilgisi siteler arası istek birlikte göndermesini engeller.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) prevents a browser from sending a cookie along with a cross-site request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-200">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ekler bir <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> özelliği, değeri olan bir <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> numaralandırma üyesi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-200">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> property whose value is a <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> enumeration member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-201">Öğenin değeri ise <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> veya <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ASP.NET ekler `SameSite` set-cookie üst öznitelik.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-201">If its value is <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> or <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ASP.NET adds the `SameSite` attribute to the set-cookie header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-202">SameSite destek uygulandığı <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> , de olarak nesneleri <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> ve <xref:System.Web.SessionState> tanımlama bilgileri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-202">SameSite support applies to <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> objects, as well as to <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies.</span></span>
 
<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-203">SameSite için ayarlayabileceğiniz bir <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> gibi nesnesi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-203">You can set SameSite for an <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> object as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var c = new HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin");
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax;
```
```vb
Dim c As New HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin")
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax
```
<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-204">SameSite tanımlama bilgileri de uygulama düzeyinde web.config dosyasını değiştirerek de yapılandırabilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-204">You can also configure SameSite cookies at the application level by modifying the web.config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <httpCookies sameSite="Strict" />
</system.web>
```
<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-205">İçin SameSite ekleyebilirsiniz <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> ve <xref:System.Web.SessionState> web yapılandırma dosyasını değiştirerek tanımlama bilgileri:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-205">You can add SameSite for <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies by modifying the web config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <authentication mode="Forms">
      <forms cookieSameSite="Lax">
         <!-- ...   -->
      </forms>
   <authentication />
   <sessionSate cookieSameSite="Lax"></sessionState>
</system.web>
```

<a name="net472" />
#### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-206">Ağ Oluşturma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-206">Networking</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-207">**Uygulama HttpClientHandler özellikleri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-207">**Implementation of HttpClientHandler properties**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-208">.NET Framework 4.7.1 sekiz özelliklerine eklenen <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler?displayProperty=nameWithType> sınıfı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-208">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 added eight properties to the <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler?displayProperty=nameWithType> class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-209">Ancak, iki belirtti bir <xref:System.PlatformNotSupportedException>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-209">However, two threw a <xref:System.PlatformNotSupportedException>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-210">.NET Framework 4.7.2 artık bu özellikleri için bir uygulama sağlar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-210">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 now provides an implementation for these properties.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-211">Özellikler şunlardır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-211">The properties are:</span></span>

- <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler.CheckCertificateRevocationList>
- <xref:System.Net.Http.HttpClientHandler.SslProtocols>

<a name="sql472" />
#### <a name="sqlclient"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-212">SQLClient</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-212">SQLClient</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-213">**Azure Active Directory Evrensel kimlik doğrulaması ve çok faktörlü kimlik doğrulaması için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-213">**Support for Azure Active Directory Universal Authentication and Multi-Factor authentication**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-214">Büyüyen uyumluluk ve güvenlik taleplerini birçok müşteri çok faktörlü kimlik doğrulaması (MFA) kullanmanızı gerektirir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-214">Growing compliance and security demands require that many customers use multi-factor authentication (MFA).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-215">Ayrıca, kullanıcı parolaları doğrudan bağlantı dizeleri dahil olmak üzere geçerli en iyi yöntemler önleyin.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-215">In addition, current best practices discourage including user passwords directly in connection strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-216">Bu değişiklikleri desteklemek için .NET Framework 4.7.2 genişletir [SQLClient bağlantı dizeleri](xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection.ConnectionString) , "Active Directory etkileşimli" MFA desteklemek varolan "Authentication" anahtar sözcüğü için yeni bir değer ekleyerek ve [Azure AD Kimlik doğrulama](/azure/sql-database/sql-database-aad-authentication-configure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-216">To support these changes, the .NET Framework 4.7.2 extends [SQLClient connection strings](xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnection.ConnectionString) by adding a new value, "Active Directory Interactive", for the existing "Authentication" keyword to support MFA and [Azure AD Authentication](/azure/sql-database/sql-database-aad-authentication-configure).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-217">Yeni etkileşimli yöntem yerel destekler ve Azure AD kullanıcıların yanı sıra Azure AD Konuk kullanıcılar federe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-217">The new interactive method supports native and federated Azure AD users as well as Azure AD guest users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-218">Bu yöntem kullanıldığında, Azure AD tarafından uygulanan MFA kimlik doğrulaması SQL veritabanları için desteklenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-218">When this method is used, the MFA authentication imposed by Azure AD is supported for SQL databases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-219">Ayrıca, kimlik doğrulama işlemi için en iyi güvenlik uygulamaları uyması için bir kullanıcı parolasını ister.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-219">In addition, the authentication process requests a user password to adhere to security best practices.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-220">SQL bağlantısı yalnızca desteklenen .NET Framework'ün önceki sürümlerinde <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryPassword?displayProperty=nameWithType> ve <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryIntegrated?displayProperty=nameWithType> seçenekleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-220">In previous versions of the .NET Framework, SQL connectivity supported only the <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryPassword?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryIntegrated?displayProperty=nameWithType> options.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-221">Bunların her ikisi de etkileşimli olmayan parçası olan [ADAL Protokolü](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-authentication-libraries), MFA desteklemiyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-221">Both of these are part of the non-interactive [ADAL protocol](/azure/active-directory/develop/active-directory-authentication-libraries), which does not support MFA.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-222">Yeni <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryInteractive?displayProperty=nameWithType> seçeneği, SQL Bağlantısı destekler MFA yanı sıra var olan kimlik doğrulama yöntemleri (parola ve tümleşik kimlik doğrulaması), kullanıcıların kullanıcı parolalarını kalıcı parolası etkileşimli olmayan bağlantı girmesine izin veren dize.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-222">With the new <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlAuthenticationMethod.ActiveDirectoryInteractive?displayProperty=nameWithType> option, SQL connectivity supports MFA as well as existing authentication methods (password and integrated authentication), which allows users to enter user passwords interactively without persisting passwords in the connection string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-223">Daha fazla bilgi ve bir örnek için "SQL--Azure AD evrensel ve çok faktörlü kimlik doğrulama desteği" bölümüne bakın [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-223">For more information and an example, see "SQL -- Azure AD Universal and Multi-factor Authentication Support" in the [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-224">**Her zaman şifreli sürüm 2 desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-224">**Support for Always Encrypted version 2**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-225">NET Framework 4.7.2 destekler, her zaman enclave tabanlı şifreli için ekler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-225">NET Framework 4.7.2 adds supports for enclave-based Always Encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-226">Her zaman şifreli özgün sürümü, şifreleme anahtarları istemci hiçbir zaman ayrılmaz bir istemci tarafı şifreleme teknolojisidir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-226">The original version of Always Encrypted is a client-side encryption technology in which encryption keys never leave the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-227">Enclave tabanlı her zaman şifreli, istemci isteğe bağlı olarak şifreleme anahtarları için SQL Server kodunu değiştirmesine olamaz, ancak, SQL Server'ın bir parçası olarak düşünülebilir güvenli bir hesaplama varlık güvenli bir enclave gönderebilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-227">In enclave-based Always Encrypted, the client can optionally send the encryption keys to a secure enclave, which is a secure computational entity that can be considered part of SQL Server but that SQL Server code cannot tamper with.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-228">Her zaman şifreli enclave tabanlı desteklemek için .NET Framework 4.7.2 aşağıdaki türleri ve üyeleri ekler <xref:System.Data.SqlClient> ad alanı:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-228">To support enclave-based Always Encrypted, the .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds the following types and members to the <xref:System.Data.SqlClient> namespace:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-229"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.EnclaveAttestationUrl?displayProperty=nameWithType>, her zaman enclave tabanlı şifreli için URI belirtir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-229"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlConnectionStringBuilder.EnclaveAttestationUrl?displayProperty=nameWithType>, which specifies the Uri for enclave-based Always Encrypted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-230"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProvider>, sağlayıcıları hangi tüm enclave türetilen soyut bir sınıf olduğu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-230"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProvider>, which is an abstract class from which all enclave providers are derived.</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-231"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlEnclaveSession>, verilen enclave oturum açmak için durum yalıtır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-231"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlEnclaveSession>, which encapsulates the state for a given enclave session.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-232"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlEnclaveAttestationParameters>, belirli bir kanıtlama protokol yürütmek için gerekli bilgileri almak için SQL Server tarafından kullanılan kanıtlama parametreleri sağlar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-232"><xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlEnclaveAttestationParameters>, which provides the attestation parameters used by SQL Server to get information required to execute a particular Attestation Protocol.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-233">Uygulama yapılandırma dosyasına sonra Özet somut uyarlamasını belirtir <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType> enclave sağlayıcısı işlevselliği sağlayan sınıf.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-233">The application configuration file then specifies a concrete implementation of the abstract <xref:System.Data.SqlClient.SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProvider?displayProperty=nameWithType> class that provides the functionality for the enclave provider.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-234">Örneğin:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-234">For example:</span></span>

```xml
<configuration>
  <configSections>
    <section name="SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProviders" type="System.Data.SqlClient.SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProviderConfigurationSection,System.Data,Version=4.0.0.0,Culture=neutral,PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089"/> 
  </configSections>
  <SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProviders>
    <providers>
      <add name="Azure" type="Microsoft.SqlServer.Management.AlwaysEncrypted.AzureEnclaveProvider,MyApp"/>
      <add name="HGS" type="Microsoft.SqlServer.Management.AlwaysEncrypted.HGSEnclaveProvider,MyApp" />
    </providers>
  </SqlColumnEncryptionEnclaveProviders >
</configuration>
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-235">Temel enclave tabanlı her zaman şifreli akışını şöyledir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-235">The basic flow of enclave-based Always Encrypted is:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-236">Kullanıcı enclave tabanlı her zaman şifreli desteklenen SQL Server bir AlwaysEncrypted bağlantısı oluşturur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-236">The user creates an AlwaysEncrypted connection to SQL Server that supported enclave-based Always Encrypted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-237">Sürücü için doğru enclave bağlanıyor emin olmak için kanıtlama hizmeti ile iletişim kurar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-237">The driver contacts the attestation service to ensure that it is connecting to right enclave.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-238">Enclave Onaylandı sonra sürücü SQL sunucusu üzerinde barındırılan güvenli enclave güvenli bir kanal kurar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-238">Once the enclave has been attested, the driver establishes a secure channel with the secure enclave hosted on SQL Server.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-239">Sürücü şifreleme anahtarlarını güvenli enclave sahip istemci tarafından SQL Bağlantısı süresince yetkili paylaşır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-239">The driver shares encryption keys authorized by the client with the secure enclave for the duration of the SQL connection.</span></span>

<a name="wpf472" />
#### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-240">Windows Presentation Foundation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-240">Windows Presentation Foundation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-241">**Kaynak tarafından ResourceDictionaries bulma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-241">**Finding ResourceDictionaries by Source**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-242">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile başlayarak, bir tanı Yardımcısı bulabilirsiniz <xref:System.Windows.Xps.Packaging.IXpsFixedPageReader.ResourceDictionaries> belirli bir kaynaktan URI oluşturuldu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-242">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, a diagnostic assistant can locate the <xref:System.Windows.Xps.Packaging.IXpsFixedPageReader.ResourceDictionaries> that have been created from a given source Uri.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-243">(Bu özellik tanılama Yardımcılar tarafından üretim uygulamaları tarafından kullanılır.) Visual Studio'nun "Düzenle-ve devam et" tesis gibi tanılama Yardımcısı çalışan uygulama değişikliklerin uygulanması amacıyla ResourceDictionary Düzenle kendi kullanıcı olanak sağlar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-243">(This feature is for use by diagnostic assistants, not by production applications.) A diagnostic assistant such as Visual Studio’s “Edit-and-Continue” facility lets its user edit a ResourceDictionary with the intent that the changes be applied to the running application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-244">Bu ulaşmada tek bir adımda çalışan uygulama şu anda düzenlenmekte sözlükten oluşturduğu tüm ResourceDictionaries bulma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-244">One step in achieving this is finding all the ResourceDictionaries that the running application has created from the dictionary that’s being edited.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-245">Örneğin, bir uygulamanın içerikleri belirli bir kaynaktan URI kopyalanır ResourceDictionary bildirebilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-245">For example, an application can declare a ResourceDictionary whose content is copied from a given source URI:</span></span>


```xml
<ResourceDictionary Source="MyRD.xaml">
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-246">Özgün biçimlendirmede düzenler bir tanılama Yardımcısı *MyRD.xaml* yeni özellik sözlük bulmak için kullanabilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-246">A diagnostic assistant that edits the original markup in *MyRD.xaml* can use the new feature to locate the dictionary.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-247">Özelliğin yeni bir statik yöntem tarafından uygulanan <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetResourceDictionariesForSource%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-247">The feature is implemented by a new static method, <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetResourceDictionariesForSource%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-248">Tanılama Yardımcısı özgün biçimlendirme tanımlayan bir mutlak URI aşağıdaki kodda gösterildiği şekilde kullanarak yeni yöntemi çağırır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-248">The diagnostic assistant calls the new method using an absolute Uri that identifies the original markup, as illustrated by the following code:</span></span>

```csharp
IEnumerable<ResourceDictionary> dictionaries = ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetResourceDictionariesForSource(new Uri("pack://application:,,,/MyApp;component/MyRD.xaml"));
```
```vb
Dim dictionaries As IEnumerable(Of ResourceDictionary) = ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetResourceDictionariesForSource(New Uri("pack://application:,,,/MyApp;component/MyRD.xaml"))
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-249">Boş bir numaralandırılabilir sürece yöntem <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> etkinleştirilir ve [ `ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO` ](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) ortam değişkeni ayarlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-249">The method returns an empty enumerable unless <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> is enabled and the [`ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) environment variable is set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-250">**ResourceDictionary sahipleri bulma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-250">**Finding ResourceDictionary owners**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-251">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile başlayarak, bir tanılama Yardımcısı sahipleri bulabilir bir verilen <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-251">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, a diagnostic assistant can locate the owners of a given <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-252">(Özellik tanılama yardımcıları ve üretim uygulamaları tarafından kullanılır.) Her bir değişiklik yapıldığında için bir <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary>, WPF otomatik olarak bulduğu tüm [DynamicResource](../wpf/advanced/dynamicresource-markup-extension.md) değişiklikten etkilenen başvuruları.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-252">(The feature is for use by diagnostic assistants and not by production applications.) Whenever a change is made to a <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary>, WPF automatically finds all [DynamicResource](../wpf/advanced/dynamicresource-markup-extension.md) references that might be affected by the change.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-253">Visual Studio'nun "Düzenle-ve devam et" tesis gibi tanılama Yardımcısı işlemek için genişletme isteyebilirsiniz [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) başvuruları.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-253">A diagnostic assistant such as Visual Studio’s “Edit-and-Continue” facility may want extend this to handle [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) references.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-254">Bu işlem ilk adımı, sözlük sahipleri bulmaktır; diğer bir deyişle, tüm nesneleri bulmak için `Resources` özelliği başvurur sözlüğe (doğrudan veya dolaylı olarak aracılığıyla <xref:System.Windows.ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries?displayProperty=nameWithType> özelliği).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-254">The first step in this process is to find the owners of the dictionary; that is, to find all the objects whose `Resources` property refers to the dictionary (either directly, or indirectly via the <xref:System.Windows.ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries?displayProperty=nameWithType> property).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-255">Üç yeni statik yöntemler üzerinde uygulanan <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics?displayProperty=nameWithType> sınıfı, her sahip temel türleri bir `Resources` özelliği, bu adımı destekler:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-255">Three new static methods implemented on the <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics?displayProperty=nameWithType> class, one for each of the base types that has a `Resources` property, support this step:</span></span>

- [`public static IEnumerable<FrameworkElement> GetFrameworkElementOwners(ResourceDictionary dictionary);`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetFrameworkElementOwners%2A)

- [`public static IEnumerable<FrameworkContentElement> GetFrameworkContentElementOwners(ResourceDictionary dictionary);`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetFrameworkContentElementOwners%2A)

- [`public static IEnumerable<Application> GetApplicationOwners(ResourceDictionary dictionary);`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.GetApplicationOwners%2A)

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-256">Kullanıcı hikayesinin sürece bu yöntem boş bir numaralandırılabilir'e dönmek. <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> etkinleştirilir ve [ `ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO` ](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) ortam değişkeni ayarlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-256">These methods return an empty enumerable unless <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> is enabled and the [`ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) environment variable is set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-257">**StaticResource başvurular bulma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-257">**Finding StaticResource references**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-258">Tanılama Yardımcısı şimdi bir bildirim almak her bir [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) başvurudur çözülmüş.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-258">A diagnostic assistant can now receive a notification whenever a [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) reference is resolved.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-259">(Özellik tanılama Yardımcılar tarafından üretim uygulamaları tarafından kullanılır.) Visual Studio'nun "Düzenle-ve devam et" tesis gibi tanılama yardımcı olan bir kaynağın tüm kullanır güncelleştirmek isteyebilirsiniz zaman değeriyle bir <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary> değişiklikler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-259">(The feature is for use by diagnostic assistants, not by production applications.) A diagnostic assistant such as Visual Studio’s “Edit-and-Continue” facility may want to update all uses of a resource when its value in a <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary> changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-260">WPF için otomatik olarak yapar [DynamicResource](../wpf/advanced/dynamicresource-markup-extension.md) başvuruyor, ancak özellikle yapmaz bunu [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) başvuruları.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-260">WPF does this automatically for [DynamicResource](../wpf/advanced/dynamicresource-markup-extension.md) references, but it intentionally does not do so for [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) references.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-261">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile başlayarak, tanılama Yardımcısı, bu kullanımları statik kaynak bulmak için bu bildirimler kullanabilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-261">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the diagnostic assistant can use these notifications to locate those uses of the static resource.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-262">Bildirim yeni tarafından uygulanan <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.StaticResourceResolved?displayProperty=nameWithType> olay:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-262">The notification is implemented by the new <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.ResourceDictionaryDiagnostics.StaticResourceResolved?displayProperty=nameWithType> event:</span></span>

```csharp
public static event EventHandler<StaticResourceResolvedEventArgs> StaticResourceResolved;
```
```vb
Public Shared Event StaticResourceResolved As EventHandler(Of StaticResourceResolvedEventArgs)
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-263">Çalışma zamanı çözümler olduğunda bu olay tetiklenir bir [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) başvuru.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-263">This event is raised whenever the runtime resolves a [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) reference.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-264"><xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.StaticResourceResolvedEventArgs> Bağımsız değişkenleri çözümleme açıklar ve nesne ve özellik barındıran belirtmek [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) başvurusu ve <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary> ve çözümlemesi için kullanılan anahtarı:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-264">The <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.StaticResourceResolvedEventArgs> arguments describe the resolution, and indicate the object and property that host the [StaticResource](../wpf/advanced/staticresource-markup-extension.md) reference and the <xref:Windows.UI.Xaml.ResourceDictionary> and key used for the resolution:</span></span>

```csharp
public class StaticResourceResolvedEventArgs : EventArgs
{
   public Object TargetObject { get; }

   public Object TargetProperty { get; }

   public ResourceDictionary ResourceDictionary { get; }

   public object ResourceKey { get; }
}
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-265">Olay oluşmaz (ve kendi `add` erişimci göz ardı edilir) sürece <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> etkinleştirilir ve [ `ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO` ](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) ortam değişkeni ayarlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-265">The event is not raised (and its `add` accessor is ignored) unless <xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics> is enabled and the [`ENABLE_XAML_DIAGNOSTICS_SOURCE_INFO`](xref:System.Windows.Diagnostics.VisualDiagnostics.GetXamlSourceInfo%2A) environment variable is set.</span></span>

<a name="clickonce472" />
#### <a name="clickonce"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-266">ClickOnce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-266">ClickOnce</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-267">HDPI kullanan uygulamalar için Office (VSTO) Windows Formları, Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) ve Visual Studio Araçları için tüm ClickOnce kullanılarak dağıtılabilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-267">HDPI-aware applications for Windows Forms, Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF), and Visual Studio Tools for Office (VSTO) can all be deployed by using ClickOnce.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-268">Dağıtım, şu girdiyi uygulama bildiriminde bulunursa, .NET Framework 4.7.2 altında başarılı olur:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-268">If the following entry is found in the application manifest, deployment will succeed under .NET Framework 4.7.2:</span></span>

```xml
<windowsSettings>
   <dpiAware xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/SMI/2005/WindowsSettings">true</dpiAware>
</windowsSettings>
```

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-269">Windows Forms uygulaması için uygulama bildirimi yerine uygulama yapılandırma dosyasına DPI tanıma ayarlama önceki geçici artık başarılı olması ClickOnce dağıtımı için gerekli değildir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-269">For Windows Forms application, the previous workaround of setting DPI awareness in the application configuration file rather than the application manifest is no longer necessary for ClickOnce deployment to succeed.</span></span>

<a name="v471"></a> 
## <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-471"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-270">.NET Framework 4.7.1 yenilikler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-270">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7.1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-271">.NET Framework 4.7.1 aşağıdaki alanlarda yeni özellikler içerir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-271">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>
 
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-272">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-272">Core</span></span>](#core471)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-273">Ortak dil çalışma zamanı (CLR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-273">Common language runtime (CLR)</span></span>](#clr)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-274">Ağ oluşturma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-274">Networking</span></span>](#net471)
- [<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-275">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-275">ASP.NET</span></span>](#asp-net471) 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-276">Ayrıca, .NET Framework 4.7.1 ana odakta yardımcı teknoloji kullanıcılar için uygun bir deneyim sağlamak üzere bir uygulamanın sağlayan iyileştirilmiş Erişilebilirlik ' dir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-276">In addition, a major focus in the .NET Framework 4.7.1 is improved accessibility, which allows an application to provide an appropriate experience for users of Assistive Technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-277">.NET Framework'teki 4.7.1 erişilebilirlik geliştirmeleri hakkında daha fazla bilgi için bkz: [erişilebilirlik .NET Framework'teki yenilikler](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-277">For information on accessibility improvements in the .NET Framework 4.7.1, see [What's new in accessibility in the .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span></span> 

<a name="core471" />
#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-278">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-278">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-279">**.NET standart 2.0 desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-279">**Support for .NET Standard 2.0**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-280">[.NET standart](~/docs/standard/net-standard.md) bir dizi standart bu sürümünü destekleyen her .NET uygulama kullanılabilir olmalıdır API tanımlar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-280">[.NET Standard](~/docs/standard/net-standard.md) defines a set of APIs that must be available on each .NET implementation that supports that version of the standard.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-281">.NET Framework 4.7.1 tam olarak .NET standart 2.0 destekler ve ekler [yaklaşık 200 API'leri](https://github.com/dotnet/standard/blob/master/netstandard/src/ApiCompatBaseline.net461.txt) .NET standart 2.0 içinde tanımlanır ve .NET Framework 4.6.1, 4.6.2 ve 4.7'eksik.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-281">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 fully supports .NET Standard 2.0 and adds [about 200 APIs](https://github.com/dotnet/standard/blob/master/netstandard/src/ApiCompatBaseline.net461.txt) that are defined in .NET Standard 2.0 and are missing from the .NET Framework 4.6.1, 4.6.2, and 4.7.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-282">(Yalnızca ek .NET standart destek dosyalarını da hedef sistemde dağıtıldıysa .NET Framework'ün bu sürümleri .NET standart 2.0 desteklediğini unutmayın.) Daha fazla bilgi için bkz: "BCL – .NET standart 2.0 desteği" [4.7.1 .NET Framework çalışma zamanının ve derleyici özellikleri](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog postası.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-282">(Note that these versions of the .NET Framework support .NET Standard 2.0 only if additional .NET Standard support files are also deployed on the target system.) For more information, see "BCL - .NET Standard 2.0 Support" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-283">**Yapılandırma oluşturucular için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-283">**Support for configuration builders**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-284">Yapılandırma oluşturucular ekleme ve uygulamalar için yapılandırma ayarlarını çalışma zamanında dinamik olarak oluşturmak geliştiriciler izin verin.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-284">Configuration builders allow developers to inject and build configuration settings for applications dynamically at run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-285">Özel yapılandırma Oluşturucular, yapılandırma bölümünde var olan verileri değiştirebilir veya tamamen sıfırdan yapılandırma bölümü oluşturmak için kullanılabilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-285">Custom configuration builders can be used to modify existing data in a configuration section or to build a configuration section entirely from scratch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-286">Yapılandırma oluşturucular olmadan .config dosyaları statik ve ayarlarını bir uygulama başlatılmadan önce biraz zaman tanımlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-286">Without configuration builders, .config files are static, and their settings are defined some time before an application is launched.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-287">Özel yapılandırma Oluşturucu oluşturmak için sizin Oluşturucu Özet türetilen <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder> sınıfı ve geçersiz kılma kendi <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessConfigurationSection%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> ve <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessRawXml%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-287">To create a custom configuration builder, you derive your builder from the abstract <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder> class and override its <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessConfigurationSection%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Configuration.ConfigurationBuilder.ProcessRawXml%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-288">Ayrıca, Oluşturucular .config dosyanızda tanımlayın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-288">You also define your builders in your .config file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-289">Daha fazla bilgi için "Yapılandırma oluşturucular" bölümüne bakın [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET ve yapılandırma özellikleri](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features) blog postası.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-289">For more information, see the "Configuration Builders" section in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 ASP.NET and Configuration Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/13/net-framework-4-7-1-asp-net-and-configuration-features) blog post.</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-290">**Çalışma zamanı özelliği algılama**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-290">**Run-time feature detection**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-291"><xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature?displayProperty=nameWithType> Sınıfı bir mekanizma sağlar önceden tanımlanmış bir özellik belirli bir .NET uygulama derleme zamanında ya da çalışma zamanında desteklenip desteklenmediğini belirlemek için.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-291">The <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature?displayProperty=nameWithType> class provides a mechanism for determine whether a predefined feature is supported on a given .NET implementation at compile time or run time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-292">Derleme zamanında bir derleyici belirtilen alan özellik desteklenip desteklenmediğini belirlemek için mevcut olup olmadığını kontrol edebilirsiniz; Öyleyse, bu özellik yararlanan kod yayma.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-292">At compile time, a compiler can check whether a specified field exists to determine whether the feature is supported; if so, it can emit code that takes advantage of that feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-293">Çalışma zamanında uygulama çağırabilirsiniz <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature.IsSupported%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> çalışma zamanında kod yayma önce yöntemi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-293">At run time, an application can call the <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.RuntimeFeature.IsSupported%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method before emitting code at runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-294">Daha fazla bilgi için bkz: [çalışma zamanı tarafından desteklenen özellikler açıklamak için yardımcı yöntemi ekleyin](https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/17116).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-294">For more information, see [Add helper method to describe features supported by the runtime](https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/17116).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-295">**Tuple türlerin seri hale getirilebilir**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-295">**Value tuple types are serializable**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-296">4.7.1, .NET Framework ile başlayan <xref:System.ValueTuple?displayProperty=nameWithType> ve onun ilişkili genel türleri olarak işaretlenmiş [Serializable](xref:System.SerializableAttribute), ikili seri hale getirme izin verir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-296">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, <xref:System.ValueTuple?displayProperty=nameWithType> and its associated generic types are marked as [Serializable](xref:System.SerializableAttribute), which allows binary serialization.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-297">Bu geçirme tanımlama grubu türleri gibi olmalısınız <xref:System.Tuple%603> ve <xref:System.Tuple%604>, değer tanımlama grubu türlerine daha kolay.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-297">This should make migrating Tuple types, such as <xref:System.Tuple%603> and <xref:System.Tuple%604>, to value tuple types easier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-298">Daha fazla bilgi için "Derleyici--ValueTuple olduğundan seri hale getirilebilir" bölümüne bakın [4.7.1 .NET Framework çalışma zamanının ve derleyici özellikleri](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog postası.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-298">For more information, see "Compiler -- ValueTuple is Serializable" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-299">**Salt okunur başvurular için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-299">**Support for read-only references**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-300">.NET Framework 4.7.1 ekler <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.IsReadOnlyAttribute?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-300">The .NET Framework 4.7.1 adds the <xref:System.Runtime.CompilerServices.IsReadOnlyAttribute?displayProperty=nameWithType>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-301">Bu öznitelik dil derleyicileri tarafından salt okunur ref dönüş türleri veya parametreleri sahip üyeler işaretlemek için kullanılır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-301">This attribute is used by language compilers to mark members that have read-only ref return types or parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-302">Daha fazla bilgi için bkz: "Derleyici--desteği için ReadOnlyReferences" [4.7.1 .NET Framework çalışma zamanının ve derleyici özellikleri](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog postası.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-302">For more information, see "Compiler -- Support for ReadOnlyReferences" in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features) blog post.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-303">Ref dönüş değerleri hakkında daha fazla bilgi için bkz: [Ref Yereller (C# Kılavuzu) dönüş değerleri ve ref](~/docs/csharp/programming-guide/classes-and-structs/ref-returns.md) ve [Ref dönüş değerleri (Visual Basic)](../../visual-basic/programming-guide/language-features/procedures/ref-return-values.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-303">For information on ref return values, see [Ref return values and ref locals (C# Guide)](~/docs/csharp/programming-guide/classes-and-structs/ref-returns.md) and [Ref return values (Visual Basic)](../../visual-basic/programming-guide/language-features/procedures/ref-return-values.md).</span></span>

<a name="clr" />
#### <a name="common-language-runtime-clr"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-304">Ortak dil çalışma zamanı (CLR)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-304">Common language runtime (CLR)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-305">**Çöp toplama performans iyileştirmeleri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-305">**Garbage collection performance improvements**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-306">Çöp toplama (GC) .NET Framework 4.7.1 yapılan değişiklikler özellikle büyük nesne yığın (LOH) ayırmaları için genel performansı iyileştirir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-306">Changes to garbage collection (GC) in the .NET Framework 4.7.1 improve overall performance, especially for Large Object Heap (LOH) allocations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-307">.NET Framework 4.7.1'da, arka plan GC (BGC) SOH yerleştirmez ortaya çıkması LOH ayırmaları sağlayan küçük nesne yığın (SOH) ve LOH ayırmalarının ayrı kilitleri kullanılır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-307">In the .NET Framework 4.7.1, separate locks are used for Small Object Heap (SOH) and LOH allocations, which allows LOH allocations to occur when Background GC (BGC) is sweeping the SOH.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-308">Sonuç olarak, çok sayıda LOH ayırmaları uygulamalar ayırma kilit çakışması ve iyileştirilmiş performans azalmasına görmeniz gerekir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-308">As a result, applications that make a large number of LOH allocations should see a reduction in allocation lock contention and improved performance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-309">Daha fazla bilgi için "Çalışma zamanı--GC performans iyileştirmeleri" bölümüne bakın [4.7.1 .NET Framework çalışma zamanının ve derleyici özellikleri](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features/) blog postası.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-309">For more information, see the "Runtime -- GC Performance Improvements" section in the [.NET Framework 4.7.1 Runtime and Compiler Features](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2017/09/28/net-framework-4-7-1-runtime-and-compiler-features/) blog post.</span></span> 

<a name="net471"/>
#### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="4e53a-310">Ağ Oluşturma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-310">Networking</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-311">**Message.HashAlgorithm SHA-2 desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-311">**SHA-2 support for Message.HashAlgorithm**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4e53a-312">.NET Framework 4.7 ve önceki sürümlerde, <xref:System.Messaging.Message.HashAlgorithm%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> desteklenen özellik değerleri <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Md5?displayProperty=nameWithType> ve <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha?displayProperty=nameWithType> yalnızca.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-312">In the .NET Framework 4.7 and earlier versions, the <xref:System.Messaging.Message.HashAlgorithm%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> property supported values of <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Md5?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha?displayProperty=nameWithType> only.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4e53a-313">4.7.1, .NET Framework ile başlayan <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha256?displayProperty=nameWithType>, <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha384?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ve <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha512?displayProperty=nameWithType> de desteklenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4e53a-313">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.1, <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha256?displayProperty=nameWithType>, <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha384?displayProperty=nameWithType>, and <xref:System.Messaging.HashAlgorithm.Sha512?displayProperty=nameWithType> are also supported.</span></span> <span
